Nations</a></strong></div></div></div></div><div class="mbl"><div class="type-break-word type-l description"><div class="rte js-description-content"><p>On January 23rd, 2020. Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus declines to declare China virus outbreak as a global health emergency. As we all know, the Coronavirus is not treatable at the moment. The number of infected and deaths has risen more than ten times (infected from 800 - close to 10,000) within only 5 days. Part of it is related to Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus under estimated the coronavirus. We strongly think Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus is not fit for his role as WHO Director General.\xc2\xa0 We call for the Immediate Resignation of Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus.</p>\n<p>A lot of us are really disappointed, we believe WHO is supposed to be political neutral. Without any investigation, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus solely believes on the death and infected numbers that the Chinese government provided with them.</p>\n<p>On the other hand, Taiwan should not be excluded from WHO for any political reasons. Their technologies are far more advanced than some of the countries on the \xe2\x80\x9cselected WHO list\xe2\x80\x9d.\xc2\xa0</p>\n<p>Please help the world to gain faith to the UN and WHO again.</p>\n<p>\xec\xb2\xad\xec\x9b\x90 \xeb\x82\xb4\xec\x9a\xa9 \xeb\xb2\x88\xec\x97\xad\xec\x9e\x85\xeb\x8b\x88\xeb\x8b\xa4. <br>1\xec\x9b\x94 23\xec\x9d\xbc \xea\xb8\xb0\xec\xa4\x80, (WHO)</p>\n<p>\xe0\xb9\x82\xe0\xb8\x9b\xe0\xb8\xa3\xe0\xb8\x94\xe0\xb8\x8a\xe0\xb9\x88\xe0\xb8\xa7\xe0\xb8\xa2\xe0\xb9\x83\xe0\xb8\xab\xe0\xb9\x89\xe0\xb8\x84\xe0\xb8\xa7\xe0\xb8\xb2\xe0\xb8\xa1\xe0\xb9\x80\xe0\xb8\x8a\xe0\xb8\xb7\xe0\xb9\x88\xe0\xb8\xad\xe0\xb8\xa1\xe0\xb8\xb1\xe0\xb9\x88\xe0\xb8\x99\xe0\xb8\xa8\xe0\xb8\xa3\xe0\xb8\xb1\xe0\xb8\x97\xe0\xb8\x98\xe0\xb8\xb2\xe0\xb8\x95\xe0\xb9\x88\xe0\xb8\xad \xe0\xb8\xad\xe0\xb8\x87\xe0\xb8\x84\xe0\xb9\x8c\xe0\xb8\x81\xe0\xb8\xb2\xe0\xb8\xa3\xe0\xb8\xaa\xe0\xb8\xab\xe0\xb8\x9b\xe0\xb8\xa3\xe0\xb8\xb0\xe0\xb8\x8a\xe0\xb8\xb2\xe0\xb8\x8a\xe0\xb8\xb2\xe0\xb8\x95\xe0\xb8\xb4 (UN) \xe0\xb9\x81\xe0\xb8\xa5\xe0\xb8\xb0 \xe0\xb8\xad\xe0\xb8\x87\xe0\xb8\x84\xe0\xb9\x8c\xe0\xb8\x81\xe0\xb8\xb2\xe0\xb8\xa3\xe0\xb8\xad\xe0\xb8\x99\xe0\xb8\xb2\xe0\xb8\xa1\xe0\xb8\xb1\xe0\xb8\xa2\xe0\xb9\x82\xe0\xb8\xa5\xe0\xb8\x81 (WHO) \xe0\xb8\x82\xe0\xb8\xad\xe0\xb8\x87\xe0\xb8\xa1\xe0\xb8\xa7\xe0\xb8\xa5\xe0\xb8\xa1\xe0\xb8\x99\xe0\xb8\xb8\xe0\xb8\xa9\xe0\xb8\xa2\xe0\xb8\x8a\xe0\xb8\xb2\xe0\xb8\x95\xe0\xb8\xb4\xe0\xb9\x84\xe0\xb8\x94\xe0\xb9\x89\xe0\xb8\x81\xe0\xb8\xa5\xe0\xb8\xb1\xe0\xb8\x9a\xe0\xb8\xa1\xe0\xb8\xb2\xe0\xb8\xad\xe0\xb8\xb5\xe0\xb8\x81\xe0\xb8\x84\xe0\xb8\xa3\xe0\xb8\xb1\xe0\xb9\x89\xe0\xb8\x87</p>\n<p>Le 23 Janvier 2020, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus n\xe2\x80\x99a pas autoris\xc3\xa9 \xc3\xa0 appliquer la cat\xc3\xa9gorisation d\xe2\x80\x99urgence sanitaire mondiale au Coronavirus chinois. Comme nous le savons, le Coronavirus n\xe2\x80\x99est pas traitable pour le moment. Le nombre d\xe2\x80\x99infect\xc3\xa9s et de morts s\xe2\x80\x99est multipli\xc3\xa9 plus de dix fois (de 800 \xc3\xa0 presque 10,000 infect\xc3\xa9s) en seulement cinq jours. Son incapacit\xc3\xa9 \xc3\xa0 reconna\xc3\xaetre et accepter le danger du virus est en partie en faute pour cela. Nous pensons sinc\xc3\xa8rement que Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus n\xe2\x80\x99est pas fait pour le r\xc3\xb4le de directeur g\xc3\xa9n\xc3\xa9ral de l\xe2\x80\x99OMS. Nous demandons sa r\xc3\xa9signation imm\xc3\xa9diate.</p>\n<p>Nous sommes vraiment d\xc3\xa9\xc3\xa7us car l\xe2\x80\x99OMS est suppos\xc3\xa9e \xc3\xaatre neutre politiquement. Pourtant, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus a accept\xc3\xa9 sans aucune enqu\xc3\xaate ni doutes les nombres fournis par le gouvernement Chinois.</p>\n<p>Qui plus est, Taiwan ne devrait pas \xc3\xaatre exclus de l\xe2\x80\x99OMS pour raisons politiques. Leurs technologies sont beaucoup plus avanc\xc3\xa9es que certains pays admis \xc3\xa0 la liste des \xc2\xab \xc3\xa9tats membres de l\xe2\x80\x99OMS \xc2\xbb.</p>\n<p>Aidons le monde \xc3\xa0 regagner confiance en l\xe2\x80\x99UN et l\xe2\x80\x99OMS.</p>\n<p>Il 23 gennaio 2020, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus ha rifiutato di dichiarare l\xe2\x80\x99epidemia virale da 2019-nCoV emergenza sanitaria globale. Come sappiamo, l\xe2\x80\x99infezione da coronavirus non \xc3\xa8 al momento trattabile. Il numero di persone affette dal virus \xc3\xa8 cresciuto esponenzialmente (da 800 a 10.000) in soli cinque giorni e continua a crescere (<a href="https://www.worldometers.info/coronavirus/" rel="nofollow">https://www.worldometers.info/coronavirus/</a> Parte di ci\xc3\xb2 \xc3\xa8 stato causato dal fatto che Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus ha deliberatamente deciso di sottostimare la pericolosit\xc3\xa0 del virus, piegandosi alle pressioni politiche della RPC. <br>Riteniamo che Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus non abbia le qualit\xc3\xa0 etiche e morali richieste per ricoprire il ruolo di Direttore Generale dell\xe2\x80\x99OMS e ne chiediamo le dimissioni immediate.<br>Molti di noi sono delusi; crediamo che l\xe2\x80\x99OMS debba essere un ente tecnico e politicamente neutro. Senza alcuna verifica scientifica indipendente, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus ha deciso di affidarsi esclusivamente ai dati di mortalit\xc3\xa0 e trasmissibilit\xc3\xa0 del virus forniti dalle autorit\xc3\xa0 cinesi, dati che, specialmente quelli forniti nelle prime fasi dell\xe2\x80\x99epidemia, si sono dimostrati palesemente falsi.<br>Sotto la direzione di Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus inoltre, Taiwan continua ad essere esclusa dall\xe2\x80\x99OMG su pressione del governo della RPC. Riteniamo che nessun popolo, per quanto piccolo e indifeso, debba essere escluso dall\xe2\x80\x99OMS.<br>Per favore, aiutateci a ristabilire la credibilit\xc3\xa0 dell\xe2\x80\x99OMS, ottenendo le dimissioni di Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus.</p>\n<p>En Enero 23 del 2020. Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus declin\xc3\xb3 declarar el brote de virus en China como una emergencia global de salud.<br>Como sabemos, el Coronavirus no es tratable en este momento. Los n\xc3\xbameros de infectados y muertos han crecido m\xc3\xa1s de diez veces (infectados desde 800 - cerca a 10,000) en s\xc3\xb3lo cuanto 5 d\xc3\xadas.<br>Una parte tiene que ver con Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus qu\xc3\xa9 subestim\xc3\xb3 el Coronavirus. Creemos fuertemente que Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus no es apto para su rol como Director General del WHO. Llamamos para la inmediata resignaci\xc3\xb3n de Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus.<br>Muchos de nosotros estamos muy decepcionados, creemos que WHO debiera ser pol\xc3\xadticamente neutral. Sin investigar, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus cree en los n\xc3\xbameros de muertos y infectados proporcionados por el gobierno de China. En la otra mano, Taiw\xc3\xa1n no debiera ser excluido del WHO por cualquier raz\xc3\xb3n pol\xc3\xadtica.<br>Sus tecnolog\xc3\xadas son muchas m\xc3\xa1s avanzadas que algunos pa\xc3\xadses en la \xe2\x80\x9clista seleccionada por WHO\xe2\x80\x9d.<br>Porfa ayuden para que el mundo pueda volver a tener fe en la UN y el WHO.</p>\n<p>\xd9\x81\xd9\x8a 23 \xd9\x83\xd8\xa7\xd9\x86\xd9\x88\xd9\x86 H\xc3\x83Y \xc4\x90\xc3\x92I \xc3\x94NG T\xe1\xbb\x94NG GI\xc3\x81M \xc4\x90\xe1\xbb\x90C TEDROS ADHANOM GHEBREYESUS T\xe1\xbb\xaa CH\xe1\xbb\xa8C NGAY L\xe1\xba\xacP T\xe1\xbb\xa8C!</p>\n<p>Xin m\xe1\xbb\x9di c\xc3\xa1c b\xe1\xba\xa1n c\xc3\xb9ng k\xc3\xbd t\xc3\xaan v\xc3\xa0o th\xe1\xbb\x89nh nguy\xe1\xbb\x87n th\xc6\xb0 d\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9bi \xc4\x91\xc3\xa2y \xc4\x91\xe1\xbb\x83 \xc4\x91\xc3\xb2i h\xe1\xbb\x8fi \xc3\xb4ng T\xe1\xbb\x95ng Gi\xc3\xa1m \xc4\x90\xe1\xbb\x91c Tedros ph\xe1\xba\xa3i t\xe1\xbb\xab ch\xe1\xbb\xa9c ngay l\xe1\xba\xadp t\xe1\xbb\xa9c.</p>\n<p><a href="http://chng.it/Sdbq8sQ7" rel="nofollow">http://chng.it/Sdbq8sQ7</a></p>\n<p>L\xe1\xbb\xaf Th\xe1\xbb\x8b T\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9dng Uy\xc3\xaan<br>Th\xe1\xbb\xa9 B\xe1\xba\xa3y, 08-02-2020</p>\n<p>~~~~~<br>N\xe1\xbb\x99i dung c\xe1\xbb\xa7a th\xe1\xbb\x89nh nguy\xe1\xbb\x87n th\xc6\xb0 t\xc3\xb4i xin t\xe1\xba\xa1m d\xe1\xbb\x8bch sang ti\xe1\xba\xbfng Vi\xe1\xbb\x87t nh\xc6\xb0 sau:</p>\n<p>\'\'K\xc3\x8aU G\xe1\xbb\x8cI \xc3\x94NG T\xe1\xbb\x94NG GI\xc3\x81M \xc4\x90\xe1\xbb\x90C T\xe1\xbb\x94 CH\xe1\xbb\xa8C Y T\xe1\xba\xbe TH\xe1\xba\xbe GI\xe1\xbb\x9aI (WHO) TEDROS ADHANOM GHEBREYESUS T\xe1\xbb\xaa CH\xe1\xbb\xa8C\'\'</p>\n<p>V\xc3\xa0o ng\xc3\xa0y 23 th\xc3\xa1ng 1 n\xc4\x83m 2020 \xc3\xb4ng Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus \xc4\x91\xc3\xa3 t\xe1\xbb\xab ch\xe1\xbb\x91i tuy\xc3\xaan b\xe1\xbb\x91 d\xe1\xbb\x8bch virus c\xe1\xbb\xa7a Trung Qu\xe1\xbb\x91c l\xc3\xa0 m\xe1\xbb\x99t tr\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9dng h\xe1\xbb\xa3p kh\xe1\xba\xa9n c\xe1\xba\xa5p cho s\xe1\xbb\xa9c kh\xe1\xbb\x8fe ng\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9di d\xc3\xa2n to\xc3\xa0n c\xe1\xba\xa7u.</p>\n<p>Nh\xc6\xb0 ch\xc3\xbang ta \xc4\x91\xc3\xa3 bi\xe1\xba\xbft, virus corona hi\xe1\xbb\x87n t\xe1\xba\xa1i kh\xc3\xb4ng th\xe1\xbb\x83 \xc4\x91i\xe1\xbb\x81u tr\xe1\xbb\x8b \xc4\x91\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\xa3c. S\xe1\xbb\x91 ng\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9di nhi\xe1\xbb\x85m v\xc3\xa0 t\xe1\xbb\xad vong \xc4\x91\xc3\xa3 t\xc4\x83ng h\xc6\xa1n m\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9di l\xe1\xba\xa7n (nhi\xe1\xbb\x85m t\xe1\xbb\xab 800 - g\xe1\xba\xa7n 10.000) ch\xe1\xbb\x89 trong 5 ng\xc3\xa0y. L\xe1\xbb\x97i m\xe1\xbb\x99t ph\xe1\xba\xa7n do \xc3\xb4ng Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus \xc4\x91\xc3\xa3 \xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9bc l\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\xa3ng sai v\xe1\xbb\x81 virus corona.</p>\n<p>Ch\xc3\xbang t\xc3\xb4i tin r\xe1\xba\xb1ng \xc3\xb4ng Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus kh\xc3\xb4ng ph\xc3\xb9 h\xe1\xbb\xa3p v\xe1\xbb\x9bi vai tr\xc3\xb2 T\xe1\xbb\x95ng gi\xc3\xa1m \xc4\x91\xe1\xbb\x91c WHO. Cho n\xc3\xaan ch\xc3\xbang t\xc3\xb4i k\xc3\xaau g\xe1\xbb\x8di \xc3\xb4ng Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus t\xe1\xbb\xab ch\xe1\xbb\xa9c ngay l\xe1\xba\xadp t\xe1\xbb\xa9c.</p>\n<p>R\xe1\xba\xa5t nhi\xe1\xbb\x81u ng\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9di trong ch\xc3\xbang t\xc3\xb4i th\xe1\xbb\xb1c s\xe1\xbb\xb1 th\xe1\xba\xa5t v\xe1\xbb\x8dng v\xe1\xbb\x81 WHO. D\xe1\xba\xabu mu\xe1\xbb\x91n tin WHO \xc4\x91\xe1\xbb\xa9ng trung l\xe1\xba\xadp v\xe1\xbb\x81 ch\xc3\xadnh tr\xe1\xbb\x8b, nh\xc6\xb0ng x\xc3\xa9t th\xe1\xba\xa5y t\xe1\xbb\x95 ch\xe1\xbb\xa9c n\xc3\xa0y kh\xc3\xb4ng m\xe1\xbb\x9f b\xe1\xba\xa5t k\xe1\xbb\xb3 cu\xe1\xbb\x99c \xc4\x91i\xe1\xbb\x81u tra n\xc3\xa0o. Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus ch\xe1\xbb\x89 bi\xe1\xba\xbft tin v\xc3\xa0o s\xe1\xbb\x91 l\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\xa3ng ng\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9di ch\xe1\xba\xbft v\xc3\xa0 ng\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9di b\xe1\xbb\x8b nhi\xe1\xbb\x85m b\xe1\xbb\x87nh do ch\xc3\xadnh ph\xe1\xbb\xa7 Trung Qu\xe1\xbb\x91c cung c\xe1\xba\xa5p.</p>\n<p>M\xe1\xba\xb7t kh\xc3\xa1c ch\xc3\xbang t\xc3\xb4i kh\xc3\xb4ng mu\xe1\xbb\x91n \xc4\x90\xc3\xa0i Loan b\xe1\xbb\x8b lo\xe1\xba\xa1i kh\xe1\xbb\x8fi WHO v\xc3\xac b\xe1\xba\xa5t k\xe1\xbb\xb3 l\xc3\xbd do ch\xc3\xadnh tr\xe1\xbb\x8b n\xc3\xa0o. C\xc3\xa1c c\xc3\xb4ng ngh\xe1\xbb\x87 c\xe1\xbb\xa7a h\xe1\xbb\x8d trong vi\xe1\xbb\x87c \xc4\x91\xe1\xbb\x91i ph\xc3\xb3 v\xe1\xbb\x9bi b\xe1\xbb\x87nh d\xe1\xbb\x8bch ti\xc3\xaan ti\xe1\xba\xbfn h\xc6\xa1n nhi\xe1\xbb\x81u so v\xe1\xbb\x9bi m\xe1\xbb\x99t s\xe1\xbb\x91 qu\xe1\xbb\x91c gia trong danh s\xc3\xa1ch WHO \xc4\x91\xc3\xa3 ch\xe1\xbb\x8dn.</p>\n<p>Xin h\xc3\xa3y gi\xc3\xbap th\xe1\xba\xbf gi\xe1\xbb\x9bi l\xe1\xba\xa5y l\xe1\xba\xa1i \xc4\x91\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\xa3c ni\xe1\xbb\x81m tin v\xc3\xa0o Li\xc3\xaan H\xe1\xbb\xa3p Qu\xe1\xbb\x91c v\xc3\xa0 WHO.\'\'</p>\n<p>23 januar 2020-te godine, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus je odbio da proglasi izbijanje kineskog virusa globalnim zdravstvenim vanrednim stanjem. Svi znamo da tretiranje korona virusa trenutno nije mogu\xc4\x87e. Broj zara\xc5\xbeenih i broj mrtvih je porastao vi\xc5\xa1e od 10 puta (zara\xc5\xbeenih od 800 do 10.000), unutar samo 5 dana. Smatramo da Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus nije sposoban da obna\xc5\xa1a poziciju generalnog direktora WHO (Svjetske zdravstvene organizacije). Pozivamo da Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus podnese hitnu ostavku.</p>\n<p>Mnogi od nas su iskreno razo\xc4\x8darani, jer vjerujemo da WHO treba biti politi\xc4\x8dki neutralan. Bez bilo kakvih dokaza ili istra\xc5\xbeivanja, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus vjeruje u broj inficiranih i mrtvih koje dobiva od kineske vlade.</p>\n<p>S druge strane, Tajvan ne treba biti isklju\xc4\x8den iz WHO, zbog bilo kakvih politi\xc4\x8dkih razloga. Njihova tehnologija je naprednija od nekih drugih zemalja koje su uklju\xc4\x8dene u WHO listu.</p>\n<p>Molim vas pomozite svijetu da ponovo ima povjerenja u UN i WHO.</p>\n<p>Am 23. Januar 2020 hat sich Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus geweigert, den Virusausbruch in China als einen globalen Gesundheitsnotstand einzustufen. Wie wir alle wissen, ist das Corona-Virus im Moment nicht behandelbar. Die Zahl der Infizierten und Toten stieg um mehr als das Zehnfache (von 800 auf nahezu 10.000 Infizierten) in nur f\xc3\xbcnf Tagen an. Ein Teil davon ist darauf zur\xc3\xbcckzuf\xc3\xbchren, dass Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus das Corona-Virus untersch\xc3\xa4tzt hat. Wir sind fest der \xc3\x9cberzeugung, dass Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus nicht geeignet f\xc3\xbcr die Rolle als Direktor der WHO ist. Wir fordern den unverz\xc3\xbcglichen R\xc3\xbccktritt von Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus.</p>\n<p>Viele von uns sind entt\xc3\xa4uscht, denn wir sind der \xc3\x9cberzeugung, dass die WHO politisch neutral sein sollte. Ohne jegliche eigenst\xc3\xa4ndige Untersuchung verl\xc3\xa4sst sich Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus blind auf die Zahlen der Infizierten und Toten von der chinesischen Regierung.</p>\n<p>Anderweitig sollte Taiwan nicht von der WHO, aufgrund politischer Gr\xc3\xbcnde, ausgeschlossen werden. Ihre Technologien sind weit fortgeschrittener als derer L\xc3\xa4nder, die auf der Liste der Ausgew\xc3\xa4hlten von der WHO stehen.</p>\n<p>Bitte helfen Sie der Welt, dass die UN und WHO an Glaubw\xc3\xbcrdigkeit wiedererlangen.</p>\n<p>\xc2\xa0</p>\n<p>2020 Janu\xc3\xa1r 23.-\xc3\xa1n a K\xc3\xadn\xc3\xa1b\xc3\xb3l sz\xc3\xa1rmaz\xc3\xb3 v\xc3\xadrus terjed\xc3\xa9s\xc3\xa9vel kapcsolatban Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus megtagadta a vil\xc3\xa1g eg\xc3\xa9szs\xc3\xa9g\xc3\xa9t befoly\xc3\xa1sol\xc3\xb3 v\xc3\xa9szhelyzet kih\xc3\xadrdet\xc3\xa9s\xc3\xa9t. K\xc3\xb6ztudott t\xc3\xa9ny, hogy az un. Koronavirusra jelenleg nincs gy\xc3\xb3gym\xc3\xb3d. A fert\xc5\x91z\xc3\xa9sek \xc3\xa9s hal\xc3\xa1loz\xc3\xa1sok sz\xc3\xa1ma a t\xc3\xadzszeres\xc3\xa9re (fert\xc5\x91z\xc3\xb6ttek sz\xc3\xa1ma 800-r\xc3\xb3l k\xc3\xb6zel 10.000-re) n\xc3\xb6vekedett mind\xc3\xb6ssze 5 nap alatt. Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesust komoly felel\xc5\x91s\xc3\xa9g terheli a Koronav\xc3\xadrus terjed\xc3\xa9s\xc3\xa9nek al\xc3\xa1becs\xc3\xbcl\xc3\xa9s\xc3\xa9ben. Er\xc5\x91s a meggy\xc5\x91z\xc5\x91d\xc3\xa9s\xc3\xbcnk abban a hitben, hogy Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus nem a megfelel\xc5\x91 szem\xc3\xa9ly a WHO (Vil\xc3\xa1g Eg\xc3\xa9szs\xc3\xa9g\xc3\xbcgyi Szervezet) f\xc5\x91igazgat\xc3\xb3i posztj\xc3\xa1ra. Ez\xc3\xa9rt k\xc3\xb6vetelj\xc3\xbck Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus azonnali lemond\xc3\xa1s\xc3\xa1t!</p>\n<p>Rengetegen vagyunk akik nem gy\xc5\x91zz\xc3\xbck kifejezni a csal\xc3\xb3dotts\xc3\xa1gunkat, hiszen WHO (Vil\xc3\xa1g Eg\xc3\xa9szs\xc3\xa9g\xc3\xbcgyi Szervezetnek) politikailag semlegesnek k\xc3\xa9ne lennie. Mindenf\xc3\xa9le vizsg\xc3\xa1lat vagy nyomoz\xc3\xa1s n\xc3\xa9lk\xc3\xbcl Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus puszta bemond\xc3\xa1sra elhitte a k\xc3\xadnai korm\xc3\xa1ny \xc3\xa1ltal k\xc3\xb6z\xc3\xb6lt adatok (fert\xc5\x91z\xc3\xa9sek \xc3\xa9s hal\xc3\xa1loz\xc3\xa1sok) val\xc3\xb3dis\xc3\xa1g\xc3\xa1t illetve a j\xc3\xa1rv\xc3\xa1ny megf\xc3\xa9kez\xc3\xa9s\xc3\xa9re hozott int\xc3\xa9zked\xc3\xa9sek eredm\xc3\xa9nyess\xc3\xa9g\xc3\xa9t.</p>\n<p>M\xc3\xa1s r\xc3\xa9szr\xc5\x91l viszont hissz\xc3\xbck, hogy Tajvant nem lehet kiz\xc3\xa1rni a WHO (Vil\xc3\xa1g Eg\xc3\xa9szs\xc3\xa9g\xc3\xbcgyi Szervezet) tagjai k\xc3\xb6z\xc3\xbcl, b\xc3\xa1rmilyen politikai okb\xc3\xb3l. Tajvan technol\xc3\xb3giai \xc3\xa9s eg\xc3\xa9szs\xc3\xa9g\xc3\xbcgi rednszere j\xc3\xb3val fejlettebb, mint n\xc3\xa9h\xc3\xa1ny tags\xc3\xa1ggal rendelkez\xc5\x91 orsz\xc3\xa1g\xc3\xa9.</p>\n<p>K\xc3\xa9r\xc3\xbcnk sz\xc3\xa9pen, hogy al\xc3\xa1\xc3\xadr\xc3\xa1soddal t\xc3\xa1mogass minket abban, hogy helyre\xc3\xa1ll\xc3\xadtsuk az ENSZ \xc3\xa9s a WHO (Vil\xc3\xa1g Eg\xc3\xa9szs\xc3\xa9g\xc3\xbcgyi Szervezet) hiteless\xc3\xa9g\xc3\xa9t.</p>\n<p>\xc2\xa0</p>\n<p>23. ledna 2020. Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus odm\xc3\xadt\xc3\xa1 prudk\xc3\xa9 \xc5\xa1\xc3\xad\xc5\x99en\xc3\xad viru v \xc4\x8c\xc3\xadn\xc4\x9b ozna\xc4\x8dit za glob\xc3\xa1ln\xc3\xad zdravotn\xc3\xad stav nouze. Jak v\xc5\xa1ichni v\xc3\xadme, koronavirus nen\xc3\xad v dan\xc3\xbd moment l\xc3\xa9\xc4\x8diteln\xc3\xbd. Po\xc4\x8det infikovan\xc3\xbdch a zem\xc5\x99el\xc3\xbdch vzrostl v\xc3\xadce ne\xc5\xbe desetkr\xc3\xa1t (z 800 infikovan\xc3\xbdch tak\xc5\x99ka na 10 000) b\xc4\x9bhem pouh\xc3\xbdch p\xc4\x9bti dn\xc3\xad. \xc4\x8c\xc3\xa1st toho se vztahuje k podcen\xc4\x9bn\xc3\xad koronaviru Tedrosem Adhanomem Ghebreyesusem. Jsme siln\xc4\x9b p\xc5\x99esv\xc4\x9bd\xc4\x8deni, \xc5\xbee Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus nen\xc3\xad zp\xc5\xafsobil\xc3\xbd pro roli gener\xc3\xa1ln\xc3\xadho \xc5\x99editele WHO. Po\xc5\xbeadujeme okam\xc5\xbeitou rezignaci Tedrose Adhanoma Ghebreyesuse.</p>\n<p>Mnoho z n\xc3\xa1s je hluboce zklaman\xc3\xbdch. V\xc4\x9b\xc5\x99\xc3\xadme, \xc5\xbee WHO by m\xc4\x9bla vystupovat politicky neutr\xc3\xa1ln\xc4\x9b. Bez jak\xc3\xa9hokoli dal\xc5\xa1\xc3\xadho \xc5\xa1et\xc5\x99en\xc3\xad se Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus spol\xc3\xa9h\xc3\xa1 slep\xc4\x9b na \xc3\xbadaje o po\xc4\x8dtech naka\xc5\xbeen\xc3\xbdch a zem\xc5\x99el\xc3\xbdch, kter\xc3\xa9 udala \xc4\x8d\xc3\xadnsk\xc3\xa1 vl\xc3\xa1da.</p>\n<p><br>D\xc3\xa1le by z WHO nem\xc4\x9bl b\xc3\xbdt vylu\xc4\x8dov\xc3\xa1n Taiwan z jak\xc3\xbdchkoli politick\xc3\xbdch d\xc5\xafvod\xc5\xaf. Jeho technologie jsou mnohem pokro\xc4\x8dilej\xc5\xa1\xc3\xad ne\xc5\xbe technologie mnoha zem\xc3\xad na \xe2\x80\x9evybran\xc3\xa9m seznamu WHO\xe2\x80\x9c.</p>\n<p><br>Pros\xc3\xadm, pomozte sv\xc4\x9btu z\xc3\xadskat znovu d\xc5\xafv\xc4\x9bru v OSN a WHO.</p>\n<p>\xc2\xa0</p>\n<p>Pada tanggal 23 Januari 2020, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus menolak untuk menyatakan wabah virus yang berasal dari Cina sebagai keadaan darurat kesehatan global. Seperti yang kita semua ketahui, coronavirus tidak dapat diobati saat ini. Jumlah yang terinfeksi dan kematian telah meningkat lebih dari sepuluh kali lipat (terinfeksi dari 800 hingga mendekati 10.000) hanya dalam 5 hari. Sebagian dari hal tersebut terjadi karena Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus meremehkan coronavirus. Kami benar-benar berpikir bahwa Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus tidak memiliki kapasitas dalam menjalankan perannya sebagai Direktur Jenderal WHO. Kami menyerukan kepada Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus untuk melakukan pengunduran diri segera.</p>\n<p>Banyak dari kita yang benar-benar merasa kecewa, kami percaya bahwa WHO seharusnya bersikap netral secara politik. Tanpa melakukan penyelidikan apa pun, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus percaya begitu saja pada jumlah kematian dan kasus yang terinfeksi yang diberikan oleh pemerintah Cina kepada mereka.</p>\n<p>Di sisi lain, Taiwan tidak boleh dikecualikan dari WHO karena alasan politik. Teknologi mereka jauh lebih maju daripada beberapa negara yang berada pada "daftar negara yang tergabung dalam WHO".</p>\n<p>Mari bantu dunia untuk mendapatkan kepercayaan kembali terhadap PBB dan WHO!</p>\n<p><br><br><br><br>*The English version shall always prevail in case of any discrepancy or inconsistency between English version and other translations.</p></div></div><div \xe0\xb8\x82\xe0\xb8\xad\xe0\xb8\x87\xe0\xb8\xa1\xe0\xb8\xa7\xe0\xb8\xa5\xe0\xb8\xa1\xe0\xb8\x99\xe0\xb8\xb8\xe0\xb8\xa9\xe0\xb8\xa2\xe0\xb8\x8a\xe0\xb8\xb2\xe0\xb8\x95\xe0\xb8\xb4\xe0\xb9\x84\xe0\xb8\x94\xe0\xb9\x89\xe0\xb8\x81\xe0\xb8\xa5\xe0\xb8\xb1\xe0\xb8\x9a\xe0\xb8\xa1\xe0\xb8\xb2\xe0\xb8\xad\xe0\xb8\xb5\xe0\xb8\x81\xe0\xb8\x84\xe0\xb8\xa3\xe0\xb8\xb1\xe0\xb9\x89\xe0\xb8\x87\\u003c/p>\\n\\u003cp>Le 23 Janvier 2020, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus n\xe2\x80\x99a pas autoris\xc3\xa9 \xc3\xa0 appliquer la cat\xc3\xa9gorisation d\xe2\x80\x99urgence sanitaire mondiale au Coronavirus chinois. Comme nous le savons, le Coronavirus n\xe2\x80\x99est pas traitable pour le moment. Le nombre d\xe2\x80\x99infect\xc3\xa9s et de morts s\xe2\x80\x99est multipli\xc3\xa9 plus de dix fois (de 800 \xc3\xa0 presque 10,000 infect\xc3\xa9s) en seulement cinq jours. Son incapacit\xc3\xa9 \xc3\xa0 reconna\xc3\xaetre et accepter le danger du virus est en partie en faute pour cela. Nous pensons sinc\xc3\xa8rement que Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus n\xe2\x80\x99est pas fait pour le r\xc3\xb4le de directeur g\xc3\xa9n\xc3\xa9ral de l\xe2\x80\x99OMS. Nous demandons sa r\xc3\xa9signation imm\xc3\xa9diate.\\u003c/p>\\n\\u003cp>Nous sommes vraiment d\xc3\xa9\xc3\xa7us car l\xe2\x80\x99OMS est suppos\xc3\xa9e \xc3\xaatre neutre politiquement. Pourtant, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus a accept\xc3\xa9 sans aucune enqu\xc3\xaate ni doutes les nombres fournis par le gouvernement Chinois.\\u003c/p>\\n\\u003cp>Qui plus est, Taiwan ne devrait pas \xc3\xaatre exclus de l\xe2\x80\x99OMS pour raisons politiques. Leurs technologies sont beaucoup plus avanc\xc3\xa9es que certains pays admis \xc3\xa0 la liste des \xc2\xab \xc3\xa9tats membres de l\xe2\x80\x99OMS \xc2\xbb.\\u003c/p>\\n\\u003cp>Aidons le monde \xc3\xa0 regagner confiance en l\xe2\x80\x99UN et l\xe2\x80\x99OMS.\\u003c/p>\\n\\u003cp>Il 23 gennaio 2020, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus ha rifiutato di dichiarare l\xe2\x80\x99epidemia virale da 2019-nCoV emergenza sanitaria globale. Come sappiamo, l\xe2\x80\x99infezione da coronavirus non \xc3\xa8 al momento trattabile. Il numero di persone affette dal virus \xc3\xa8 cresciuto esponenzialmente (da 800 a 10.000) in soli cinque giorni e continua a crescere (\\u003ca href=\\"https://www.worldometers.info/coronavirus/\\" rel=\\"nofollow\\">https://www.worldometers.info/coronavirus/\\u003c/a> Parte di ci\xc3\xb2 \xc3\xa8 stato causato dal fatto che Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus ha deliberatamente deciso di sottostimare la pericolosit\xc3\xa0 del virus, piegandosi alle pressioni politiche della RPC. \\u003cbr>Riteniamo che Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus non abbia le qualit\xc3\xa0 etiche e morali richieste per ricoprire il ruolo di Direttore Generale dell\xe2\x80\x99OMS e ne chiediamo le dimissioni immediate.\\u003cbr>Molti di noi sono delusi; crediamo che l\xe2\x80\x99OMS debba essere un ente tecnico e politicamente neutro. Senza alcuna verifica scientifica indipendente, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus ha deciso di affidarsi esclusivamente ai dati di mortalit\xc3\xa0 e trasmissibilit\xc3\xa0 del virus forniti dalle autorit\xc3\xa0 cinesi, dati che, specialmente quelli forniti nelle prime fasi dell\xe2\x80\x99epidemia, si sono dimostrati palesemente falsi.\\u003cbr>Sotto la direzione di Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus inoltre, Taiwan continua ad essere esclusa dall\xe2\x80\x99OMG su pressione del governo della RPC. Riteniamo che nessun popolo, per quanto piccolo e indifeso, debba essere escluso dall\xe2\x80\x99OMS.\\u003cbr>Per favore, aiutateci a ristabilire la credibilit\xc3\xa0 dell\xe2\x80\x99OMS, ottenendo le dimissioni di Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus.\\u003c/p>\\n\\u003cp>En Enero 23 del 2020. Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus declin\xc3\xb3 declarar el brote de virus en China como una emergencia global de salud.\\u003cbr>Como sabemos, el Coronavirus no es tratable en este momento. Los n\xc3\xbameros de infectados y muertos han crecido m\xc3\xa1s de diez veces (infectados desde 800 - cerca a 10,000) en s\xc3\xb3lo cuanto 5 d\xc3\xadas.\\u003cbr>Una parte tiene que ver con Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus qu\xc3\xa9 subestim\xc3\xb3 el Coronavirus. Creemos fuertemente que Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus no es apto para su rol como Director General del WHO. Llamamos para la inmediata resignaci\xc3\xb3n de Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus.\\u003cbr>Muchos de nosotros estamos muy decepcionados, creemos que WHO debiera ser pol\xc3\xadticamente neutral. Sin investigar, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus cree en los n\xc3\xbameros de muertos y infectados proporcionados por el gobierno de China. En la otra mano, Taiw\xc3\xa1n no debiera ser excluido del WHO por cualquier raz\xc3\xb3n pol\xc3\xadtica.\\u003cbr>Sus tecnolog\xc3\xadas son muchas m\xc3\xa1s avanzadas que algunos pa\xc3\xadses en la \xe2\x80\x9clista seleccionada por WHO\xe2\x80\x9d.\\u003cbr>Porfa ayuden para que el mundo pueda volver a tener fe en la UN y el WHO.\\u003c/p>\\n\\u003cp>\xd9\x81\xd9\x8a 23 Ghebreyesus recusou declarar o surto do Coronavirus nCoV-2019 como uma emerg\xc3\xaancia de sa\xc3\xbade global. Como sabemos, o Coronavirus n\xc3\xa3o \xc3\xa9 trat\xc3\xa1vel at\xc3\xa9 o momento. O n\xc3\xbamero de infectados e mortes subiu mais de dez vezes (infectatos de 800 - perto de 10000) em meros 5 dias. Parte disto \xc3\xa9 ligado a Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus subestimando o Coronavirus. \xc3\x89 nossa firme opini\xc3\xa3o que Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus n\xc3\xa3o \xc3\xa9 apto para atuar como o Diretor Geral da WHO. Chamamos para a ren\xc3\xbancia imediata de Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus.\\u003cbr>Muitos de n\xc3\xb3s estamos extremamente desapontados, acreditamos que a WHO deve ser politicamente neutra. Sem nenhuma investiga\xc3\xa7\xc3\xa3o, Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus acredita plenamente nos n\xc3\xbameros de mortes e infectados que o governo Chin\xc3\xaas prov\xc3\xaam. \\u003cbr>Por outro lado, Taiwan n\xc3\xa3o deve ser excl\xc3\xbaida da WHO por qualquer raz\xc3\xa3o pol\xc3\xadtica.
